xemacs-packages-extra in epel-8

This page displays detail informations of the xemacs-packages-extra package. You might want go back to the main page of xemacs-packages-extra.

Changelog

Date Author Change
2019-12-12 Jerry James - 20191207-1 - Update to the latest cc-mode and time packages
2019-10-01 Jerry James - 20190315-3 - New texinfo version assumes UTF-8 input, so convert ISO8859-1 texinfo files
2019-07-27 Fedora Release Engineering - 20190315-2 - Rebuilt for https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Fedora_31_Mass_Rebuild
2019-03-23 Jerry James - 20190315-1 - Update all packages - Include mew again, since xemacs-mew no longer exists - Add -python3 patch and build with python3 instead of python2 - Add -eval-when and -deps patches to fix FTBFS
2019-02-03 Fedora Release Engineering - 20171219-4 - Rebuilt for https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Fedora_30_Mass_Rebuild
2018-07-14 Fedora Release Engineering - 20171219-3 - Rebuilt for https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Fedora_29_Mass_Rebuild
2018-02-09 Fedora Release Engineering - 20171219-2 - Rebuilt for https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Fedora_28_Mass_Rebuild
2017-12-29 Jerry James - 20171219-1 - Update cc-mode, edit-utils, prog-modes, and time
2017-08-05 Jerry James - 20170330-1 - Update all packages, especially CC-Mode to fix FTBFS
2017-08-05 Jerry James - 20170114-4 - Fix xemacs(bin) dependency - Eliminate dependencies on /usr/bin/env
